<script>
$(document).on('ready', function() {
  Plus = window.Plus || {} ;
  Plus.cart = {};

  var ajaxSuccessFn = function(action) {
    var itemCount,
      $cartTargetDesktop = $('#cart-target-desktop'),
      $cartTargetMobile = $('#cart-target-mobile');

    if (typeof(action) === 'function') {
      action();
    } else if (action !== null) {
      switch(action) {
        case 'reload':
          location.reload();
          break;
        case 'checkout':
          window.location = '/checkout';
          break;
        case 'update':
          // Update these selectors per theme
          itemCount = Plus.cart.return("item_count");
          $cartTargetDesktop.text(itemCount);
          $cartTargetMobile.text(itemCount);
          break;
        default:
          // nothing
          console.warn('Unrecognized value for action parameter: ' + action);
      }
    }
  };

  Plus.cart.update = function(data_val, variant_qty, action) {
    var dataObject = {},
      productObject = {};

    // Create an object to pass as ajax data
    if (typeof(variant_qty) === 'number') {
      productObject[data_val] = variant_qty;
      dataObject.updates = productObject;
    } else {
      dataObject = data_val;
    }

    $.ajax({
      // async: false for functions that rely on this finishing first
      async: false,
      type: 'POST',
      url: '/cart/update.js',
      data: dataObject,
      dataType: 'json',
      error: function() {
        console.log('Ajax request failed.');
      }
    })
    .complete(function(response) {
      if (response.status === 200) {
        ajaxSuccessFn(action);
      }
    });
  };

  Plus.cart.change = function(cart_object, action) {
    $.ajax({
      // async: false for functions that rely on this finishing first
      async: false,
      type: 'POST',
      url: '/cart/change.js',
      data: cart_object,
      dataType: 'json',
      error: function() {
        console.log('Ajax request failed.');
      }
    })
    .complete(function(response) {
      if (response.status === 200) {
        ajaxSuccessFn(action);
      }
    });
  };

  Plus.cart.return = function(key, cart_items) {
    if (cart_items) {
      // Make an array based on the 'key'
      $.ajax({
        // async: false so Plus.cart.array can be updated before returning
        async: false,
        type: 'GET',
        url: '/cart.js',
        dataType: 'json',
        success: function (data) {
          var data_items = data.items,
            cart_arr = [];

          for (var i = 0, dataItemsLength = data_items.length; i < dataItemsLength; i++) {
            cart_arr.push(data_items[i][key]);
          }

          Plus.cart.array = cart_arr;
        }
      });

      if (typeof Plus.cart.array[0] !== 'undefined') {
        return Plus.cart.array;
      } else {
        console.log('Could not retrieve any cart items with "' + key + '" as the key.');
      }
    } else if (key === 'data') {
      // Console log everything that is in the cart object
      $.ajax({
        type: 'GET',
        url: '/cart.js',
        dataType: 'json',
        success: function(data) {
          console.log(data);
        }
      });
    } else {
      // Return the value of a single cart property
      $.ajax({
        // async: false so Plus.cart.value can be updated before returning
        async: false,
        type: 'GET',
        url: '/cart.js',
        dataType: 'json',
        success: function (data) {
          Plus.cart.value = data[key];
        }
      });

      if (typeof Plus.cart.value !== "undefined") {
        return Plus.cart.value;
      } else {
        console.log('Could not retrieve any cart data with "' + key + '" as the key.');
      }
    }
  };

  Plus.cart.item = function(value, property, criteria) {
    var criteria_met,
      crit_key,
      item_key;

    //Returning 'value' where all criteria is true.
    //e.g. Plus.cart.item('quantity',false,{id:123456, properties.Gift wrapped : 400})
    // Return the quantity of cart items whose id is 123456 and 'Gift wrapped' property is 400
    Plus.cart.itemValue = undefined;

    $.ajax({
      // async: false for functions that rely on this finishing first
      async: false,
      type: 'GET',
      url: '/cart.js',
      dataType: 'json',
      success: function (data) {
        var data_items = data.items;

        for(var i = 0, dataItemsLength = data_items.length; i < dataItemsLength; i++) {
          criteria_met = true;

          for (var key in criteria) {
            if (criteria.hasOwnProperty(key)) {

              if (!criteria_met) {
                break;
              } else {
                if (key === 'properties' && data_items[i].properties) {
                  for (var prop in criteria.properties) {
                    if (data_items[i].properties[prop] !== null) {
                      crit_key = criteria.properties[prop];
                      item_key = data_items[i].properties[prop];
                    } else {
                      criteria_met = false;
                      break;
                    }
                  }
                } else {
                  crit_key = criteria[key];
                  item_key = data_items[i][key];
                }

                if (crit_key === item_key) {
                  criteria_met = true;
                } else {
                  criteria_met = false;
                }
              }
            }

            if (criteria_met) {
              if (property) {
                //If we're looking for a property
                Plus.cart.itemValue = data_items[i].properties[value];
                break;
              } else {
                Plus.cart.itemValue = data_items[i][value];
                break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });

    if (typeof Plus.cart.itemValue !== 'undefined') {
      return Plus.cart.itemValue;
    } else {
      console.log('Could not retrieve any cart item with the given criteria.');
    }
  };
});
</script>



<script>

(function($){

  var qtyClass = '.js-qty-num';
  var ajaxQtyClass = '.sitecart-qty-num';
  var cartQtyClass = '.cart-product-qty';
  var cartMax = 2 || 4;

  

  $(document).on('ready',function(){

    // Add fallback 'max' data attributes to quantites
    $(qtyClass).attr('max',cartMax);
    $(ajaxQtyClass).attr('max',cartMax);
    $(cartQtyClass).attr('max',cartMax);

    var qtyCheckFn = function(e, itemQuantity, initElem, $initElemParent) {

      // Define trigger element
      var $initElem = $(initElem);

      // Is item quantity greater than defined max
      if (itemQuantity >= cartMax && $initElem.data('limitadjust')) {
        e.preventDefault();

        // Is trigger element a number input? Yes? Reset value to defined max
        if ($(initElem).is("[type='number']") ) {
          $initElem.val(cartMax);
        };

        // Show tooltip message
        $initElemParent.removeClass('warning--hide');
        setTimeout(function(){
          $initElemParent.addClass('warning--hide');
        }, 2000);
      };

    };

    

    

  })

})(jQuery)

</script>

<!-- Change blog url script for kids -->
<script>
  setInterval(function(){
    var location = window.location.href;
    var loc_split = location.split('/');
    var last_val = loc_split[loc_split.length-1];
    if(last_val == 'kids'){
    	$('.blog-main-link').attr('href','/blogs/lookbooks-kids');
    }else{
        $('.blog-main-link').attr('href','/blogs/news');
    }
    
  },1000);
</script>

<script>
$(window).scroll(function() {
   $('.js-ksplash-header-altdropdown').removeClass('is-active');
   $('.js-ksplash-header-main-links-item').removeClass('is-hover');
});  

$('ksplash-header-main-link').click(function() {
  if ($('js-ksplash-header-main-links-item')) {
    $('.js-ksplash-header-main-links-item').addClass('is-hover');
  } else if ($('js-ksplash-header-main-links-item is-hover')) {
    $('.js-ksplash-header-main-links-item').removeClass('is-hover');
  }
});
</script>

      $('.accordion-header').on('click', function(){
        if($(this).parent().hasClass('expand')){
          $(this).parent().find('.accordion-content').slideUp();
          $(this).parent().removeClass('expand').find('.expand').removeClass('expand');
        }else{
          $(this).parent().addClass('expand');
          $(this).siblings('.accordion-content').slideDown();
          $(this).parent().siblings('.expand').find('.accordion-content').slideUp();
          $(this).parent().siblings('.expand').removeClass('expand').find('.expand').removeClass('expand');
        }
      })
    })
  </script>

x.parentNode.insertBefore(s, x);
})();
</script>
<!-- END KLAVIYO SIGNUP FORM CODE -->

</body>
</html>
